# <a name="encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="98d2a-103">加密鏈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98d2a-103">Encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="98d2a-104">Office 365 利用許多不同的憑證提供者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98d2a-104">Office 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="98d2a-105">下列說明當存取 Office 365 時，使用者可能會遇到的已知 Office 365 根憑證的完整清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98d2a-105">The following describes the complete list of known Office 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="98d2a-106">如需您可能需要在自己的基礎結構中安裝之憑證的詳細資訊，請參閱[Plan For Office 365 的協力廠商 SSL 憑證](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98d2a-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="98d2a-107">下列憑證資訊適用于 Office 365 的所有全球和國內雲端實例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98d2a-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Office 365.</span></span>

>[!NOTE]
><span data-ttu-id="98d2a-108">如需適用于**DOD 和 Gcc 高級**客戶的憑證資訊，請參閱[Office 365 加密鏈-DOD 和 gcc high](encryption-office-365-certificate-chains-itar.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98d2a-108">For certificate information that applies to **DOD and GCC High** customers, see [Office 365 encryption chains - DOD and GCC High](encryption-office-365-certificate-chains-itar.md).</span></span>
